I came here to get my first tattoo. The first time I came for just an outline of a symbol. The lines came out uneven, like a part of it was thicker than the rest. I'm not sure if it was my fault that the ink bled because I put a shirt over it right away. I wasn't given any sheet or tips on aftercare either, but I should've asked. Then a couple of months later I decided I wanted the symbol filled in and a little extra added to it. So I come back. I noticed after it healed that there are patches of my skin I can still see. I asked for it to be filled in completely. I know it's not my fault this time because my husband had a sheet he got from a different tattoo studio with the aftercare and we did everything it said. Now I'm just really bummed about my not well done first tattoo and I'm going to have to spend more money to get it done right, but definitely elsewhere. The staff seemed friendly, the shop was really cool but I just feel that they rushed doing my tattoo. :(</text>

< Review>
Everyone is always nice to me, i used to pop in late at night after work and even though they were usually stocking shelves someone would always check me out quickly. I feel that if i asked someone politely to watch me walk to my car they wouldn't mind. During the day i think the staff works very hard and the location attracts some undesirable shoppers, so if they ever seem short or "rude" it's probably because they had to handle a lousy situation. The photo center is just fine; sometimes it takes longer than an hour for pickup, but for myself i don't mind. I've never used the pharmacy so i can't comment on that. Overall, for a quick stop at a local drug store, this is a fine place to go. Just realize employees spend their day on their feet, the place is always busy and some dirty individuals come in and harass them; so if they aren't peppy perhaps take a moment to say, "thank you and have a good day", a little kindness can go a long way.</Review>

<username>Chris Woodcox aka Alpine</username>< text>
I have played this course countless times. The views are beautiful and the course is well maintained. It offers a number of fun and challenging holes (18 in all). I had began going up there years ago prior to the city stepping in and upgrading the course. A grant was provided to add chain baskets which would replace the older tone poles. Also added were concrete slabs and directional arrows at the beginning of every hole. I try to get up there as often as I can and enjoy it every time! Disc golf is one of the funnest Sports around in my opinion.</text>

Seeing this  Olga yelled at by wife to go in the water and get him out  and snatched my one year old from her hand. A woman named Melissa had me sign in and informed me she had no appointments available the rest of the day, even though I didn't ask for one. She asked if I knew what I was looking for, and I said a wedding dress, but I just wanted to look. Told her I had received an email from David's Bridal that advertised a big September sale with dresses as low as $99. She pointed to where they were and another woman that worked there walked over. Melissa said, This is Michelle, and she's looking for a $99 dress. Well, the woman she told that to didn't seem to care. And that made me angry because I didn't tell Melissa I was looking for a $99 dress! I mentioned the email I received, and stated I just wanted to look! Then I started to ask a question, but Melissa saw a man outside that was about to walk in, and she rudely told the other saleswoman something about him right in front of me but was speaking through her teeth and staring at him as he was walking in it a small bag as if he was going to return something. I stopped talking so that Melissa could finish saying whatever she was saying about that man as he was walking in. I thought that was very rude and unprofessional. Anyway, I  finally asked my question, Melissa answered it, and I  went to look at the wedding dresses. I saw a few dresses I liked, but decided I'd rather make an appointment at a different store, and give them my business instead because of how rude Melissa was. She made a very bad first impression with me. As I said, I've never been there before, I didn't know you have to make an appointment to look at dresses even if you're not there to buy it that day, I don't like how she was talking about a man that was walking into the store as if he was about to annoy them or they didn't want to help him, and I didn't want to ask either of them any questions because I didn't want to annoy them since I didn't have an appointment. I walked all over the store, and no one said a word to me the whole time. Finally I decided to leave, and not one person said goodbye to me. What a terrible first impression, and what a terrible experience I had my first time ever at David's Bridal. I hope the next one I go to doesn't have such horrible service.</Text>
